\texttt{> go to cellar} \\
\texttt{You are in a cellar now. There are a green beetle, a spiderweb, a bucket of ectoplasm, a red beetle, a spider egg and a spider. The green beetle is on the floor. The spiderweb is on the floor. The bucket of ectoplasm is on the floor. The red beetle is on the floor. The spider egg is on the floor. The spider is on the floor. There is a passage to a hallway here.} \\
\texttt{> take spider egg} \\
\texttt{You take the spider egg. In your inventory you have a peach and a spider egg.} \\
\texttt{> go to hallway} \\
\texttt{You are in a hallway now. There are passages to a bedroom, a magic workshop, a reading room and a broom closet here.} \\
\texttt{> go to magic workshop} \\
\texttt{You are in a magic workshop now. There are a workbench, a orrery, a fire wand, a fairy wand and a zulpowand. The fire wand is on the ceiling. The fairy wand is on the ceiling. The zulpowand is on the ceiling. There are passages to a kitchen and a bedroom here.} \\
\texttt{Magical experiments have reversed and dampened gravity in this room. You begin to float in the air.} \\
\texttt{> go to kitchen} \\
\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a ice wand, a borpulus, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a liquid. The ice wand is on the floor. The borpulus is on the floor. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
            }
        }
    }
    & & \\ \\

\texttt{> go to kitchen} \\
\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\

\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
\texttt{I don't know what you mean.} \\

\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\

\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
\texttt{I don't know what you mean.} \\

\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\

\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
\texttt{I don't know what you mean.} \\

\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\

\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
\texttt{I don't know what you mean.} \\

\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\

\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
\texttt{I don't know what you mean.} \\

\texttt{You are in a kitchen now. There are a borpulus, a liquid, a cupboard, a cauldron, a counter, a plate and a ice wand. The borpulus is on the floor. The liquid is in the cauldron. The cupboard is closed. The cauldron is on the floor. The plate is on the floor. The ice wand is on the floor. There are passages to a conservatory and a pantry here.} \\
\texttt{Gravity behaves normally in this room. You stop floating in the air.} \\
\texttt{> put spider egg in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The spider egg is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The spider egg absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a snap.} \\
\texttt{> put peach in cauldron} \\
\texttt{The peach is now in the cauldron.} \\
\texttt{The peach absorbs into the liquid in the cauldron with a crackle.} \\
\texttt{The liquid in the cauldron starts to glow.} \\
\texttt{You have successfully brewed Rincewind's potion.} \\
\texttt{> done} \\
\texttt{You have achieved your goal. Congratulations!} \\
\texttt{Thank you for playing.} \\
